◎ Zhang Zhen Retreated to Zhao'an Again 95

▲ Red Bandits Set Up Bases in Western and Southern Fujian

▲ And Actively Explore Tong'an and Zhangpu Separately

Fuzhou Correspondence: The southwest half of Fujian Province has now become the sphere of influence of the Red Bandits. Changting, Liancheng, Longyan, Nan Jing, Longxi, Haicheng, Wuping, Shanghang, Yongding and nine counties have been completely lost. Qingliu, Ninghua, Chong'an, Pucheng, Tong'an and Pinghe are in contention between the government and the bandits. Currently, the bandits have established a base in western Fujian in Changting, where the Soviet Government of Western Fujian and the headquarters of the Seventh Red Army are located, governing Liancheng (Tingzhou), Wuping, Shanghang, and Yongding counties. They have established a base in southern Fujian in Longxi (Zhangzhou), where the Soviet Government of Southern Fujian and the headquarters of the First Red Army Corps are located, governing Longyan, Nan'jing, Haicheng, and Tong'an counties. They are registering households, labeling houses, arresting local gentry and merchants in Zhangzhou City, and distributing money looted from organs and wealthy families to workers and peasants, encouraging them to join the Red Army. Regarding military operations, they are still taking a defensive stance towards Tong'an, holding out with Chen Guohui's brigade of the government army between Jiangdong Bridge, Jiaowei, and Fan. There have been no major changes in recent days. However, people's hearts are very restless in Quanzhou and Tong'an. They are relocating to the countryside, shops are closing, and schools are suspended, making the local area quite chaotic. The situation in Zhangpu is still extremely urgent. Day after day, the Zhangzhou bandits have been setting off in that direction in an endless stream. It is said that the bandits are making a full-scale advance on Zhangpu, advancing from Nan'jing and Haicheng. The government troops in Zhangpu only have one regiment of Zhang Zhen's division, so the situation is also very critical. People are fleeing to Yunxiao, Zhao'an, and Dongshan, and the order is very chaotic. However, according to news from the Security Office, as of the 27th, Zhang's division was still deploying defenses in Zhangpu City and the surrounding suburbs. The rumors of its loss are still difficult to confirm. Zhang Zhen himself originally led a large force in Yunxiao, but now, due to the emergency in Zhangpu, he retreated to Zhao'an again to deploy defenses the day before yesterday. According to Zhang Zhen's telegram to the province, there are about 6,000 people gathered in Zhangpu, Yunxiao, and Zhao'an, and he is planning to hold on and wait for reinforcements. However, in terms of geography, Yunxiao is behind Zhangpu, and Zhao'an is behind Yunxiao. Now that Zhang is retreating further and further back, it is really unpredictable. As for the Guangdong army's support for Fujian, it was originally divided into three routes: the left wing was undertaken by Huang Renhuan's department of the First Independent Division, and Xie Zheng and Ouyang Xin's two regiments of the Eighth Division, and Zhong Shaokui's department of the Newly Compiled First Independent Brigade, entering Wuping from Jiaoling and advancing to Shanghang. The central route was undertaken by Guo Hui and Zhao Lan's two regiments of the Third Army's Training Regiment, entering Fengshi from Dapu and advancing to Yongding. The right wing was undertaken by Huang Tingzhen's department of the Eighth Division, entering Pinghe and Zhao'an from Raoping. At present, only the left wing is advancing into Wuping and Shanghang. The middle and right wings have not yet moved, so they have not been able to make contact immediately. In addition, Fang Shengtao, Chairman of the Provincial Government, Liu Tong, the newly appointed Director of the Civil Affairs Department, He Gongsan, the former Director of the Finance Department, and Jiang Pingfan of the Provincial Committee arrived in the province on April 28. It is said that the specific methods for both the bandit suppression and financial problems have been discussed with the central government during this trip to Beijing. The detailed plan will be recorded again later. (April 29)

◎ Gao You Tang Impeaches Liu Ruiheng 97

▲ Because Liu Deceived the Government to Form a Tobacco Prohibition Office

▲ In Name, Tobacco Prohibition, But in Reality, Openly Selling Tobacco

The Supervisory Committee member, Gao You Tang, submitted an impeachment against Liu Ruiheng, stating: "Regarding the matter of impeachment, opium's harm to China is worse than floods and fierce beasts. The government, recognizing this, specifically established the Tobacco Prohibition Committee and promulgated the Tobacco Prohibition Punishment Law, which is stricter than the Criminal Law. This shows that the government attaches importance to tobacco prohibition and is determined. Unexpectedly, Liu Ruiheng, the Chairman of the Tobacco Prohibition Committee and concurrently the Director of the Department of Health, has achieved little since taking office, and his performance has greatly declined compared to the era of Zhang Zhijiang, which already constitutes negligence of duty. What is even more astonishing is that he dared to deceive the government and organize the Tobacco Prohibition Investigation Office. The regulations he formulated completely destroyed the powers of the judiciary, administration, and police, handling everything single-handedly. He stipulated that a certain amount of tax would be levied on each tael of opium, calling it tobacco prohibition, but in reality, it was selling tobacco. The directors of the investigation offices he dispatched to various provinces all paid a heavy price. Within less than ten days of opening, they extorted recklessly, and the voices of opposition filled the country. Only then did the government strictly order its cancellation. However, the planting of tobacco in various provinces continued as before, the transportation of tobacco continued as before, the selling of tobacco continued as before, and the smoking of tobacco continued as before. The government's orders were equal to nothing. Liu Ruiheng was not only as deaf and blind, but also tacitly approved the planting, transportation, selling, and smoking of tobacco as a personal opportunity to make money, hoping to make a comeback and revive. People are talking about it, and it is not without reason. The Tobacco Prohibition Law has been promulgated for a long time, how could Liu Ruiheng not know? Yet, he was completely heartless, using his power to openly sell tobacco. The ridicule of various countries was unheard of, and the health of the people was not taken into account. There is nothing more harmful to the country and the people than this. Liu Ruiheng has violated Article 16 and Article 18 of the Tobacco Prohibition Law and is hereby impeached according to the law. Please hand over Liu Ruiheng, the Chairman of the Tobacco Prohibition Committee and concurrently the Director of the Department of Health, for disciplinary action. The criminal part should be transferred to the court for trial. It is also hoped that the government will strictly prohibit the disguised selling of tobacco in the future and not take measures that are like drinking poison to quench thirst, so as to preserve the dignity of the country. It is a great fortune." (April 28th)

◎ Repeated Bombing Cases in Guangzhou 98

▲ The Reason is That Bandits Extorted Money Unsuccessfully

Guangzhou Correspondence: Robbers and bandits in Guangzhou have been rampant in recent days, repeatedly sending letters to various shops extorting huge sums of money. Those who do not comply are harassed by bombs. Initially, the targets of extortion were the various river ferry companies, so the bombing of ships by bandits has been heard of from time to time. Unexpectedly, two bombing incidents causing injuries have occurred recently. One was near the Daji Coal Factory behind the Doufuyong in Huadishan Village. On the morning of the 20th, a huge bomb suddenly exploded, piercing more than a dozen large holes in the wall of the factory's machine department, each hole about a foot wide, and the smaller ones also several inches. Eight windows were completely destroyed. The wooden roots of the fence outside the wall were also completely broken. The broken shell pieces flew to the vicinity, collapsing several pieces of the house wall and injuring the back and feet. After the incident, the military police arrived at the scene to investigate and found a piece of shrapnel more than eight minutes thick, which shows the size of the bomb. At the same time, a manifesto from the bandit leader Liang Gaozhong was found near the corner of a new house, the wording of which was absurd and nothing more than a statement that the extortion was unsuccessful and the bomb was used as a warning. The other incident occurred on the same evening at the Zhongshan Cinema on Xiajiupu Road in Xiguan, where a bombing incident by bandits injured people. On that evening, a guest named Chen Jia, accompanied by his friend Liang Yi, took a seat in the third row of ordinary seats in the theater. Suddenly, they noticed an iron can under the seat, wrapped in paper. Chen did not know what it was and initially did not expect it to be a bomb planted by bandits. When he touched it with his hand, a loud noise suddenly erupted. All five fingers of Chen's left hand were blown off, and blood flowed like a stream. His lower scrotum was also blown open. Chen fainted from the extreme pain, and his injuries were very serious. After the explosion, the entire theater was in chaos. The police and military police rushed to the scene after hearing the alarm and searched among the crowd for a long time, but did not find any suspects. They then sent the injured person to the hospital for treatment. However, Chen died only forty minutes after arriving at the hospital due to his serious injuries. After the incident, a bandit letter was found in the hospital, which briefly stated that the matter requested from the theater had been ignored, so the smallest means of punishment were used. If they continued to refuse to hand it over, more violent bombings would be used, and so on. It was signed by Liao Jiruo of the Guangdong Tianyi Hall. It is heard that the theater had repeatedly received extortion letters from Liao before, but the person in charge regarded them as intimidation and ignored them. Unexpectedly, in a prosperous area with the military police standing everywhere, the bandits would actually dare to do this. (April 21st evening)

◎ Establishment of the Jiangsu Provincial War Zone Relief Association 99

▲ And Election of Standing Committee Members

Due to the outbreak of the war against Japan, the counties of Baoshan, Taicang, and Jiading in Jiangsu Province have fallen into the war zone and suffered severely. The people have been killed, injured, and displaced. The counties in the vicinity of the war zone have also suffered significant military losses indirectly. The government should take measures to provide relief, but the treasury is empty and the economic capacity is weak. The problems of current relief, future rehabilitation, and recovery must be solved by pooling the financial and human resources of the entire province. Therefore, the War Zone Relief Association was specifically organized in order to gather the strengths of all parties. After months of preparation, the members were appointed, and the inaugural meeting was held in the provincial government on April 28th. The details are recorded as follows:

▲ The attending members were Zhu Zhongjing, Yin Zhaorong, Zhu Yuanzhi, Guo Songru, Ma Yintang, Cai Zhaozhai, Qian Yizhen, Guo Junfu, Zhao Songping, Huang Zhenhuan, Wang Yibai, Liu Xuzhou, Qian Sunqing, Gao Jiansi, Xue Mingjian, Han Guojun, Xu Dingkang, Zhu Shaowen, Wang Shuxiang, Cheng Jingsheng, Jiang Wenyu, Ma Junqing, Zhang Yipeng, Shi Kuihe, Shen Baoyi, Dong Zengru, Liu Zhiren, Sun Shaojiang, Wang Boqiu, Wang Zhanwei, Ni Zhuhua, Xia Langyun, Yan Suiqiu, Chen Xinming, Liu Zaiji, Wang Qihua, Dai Boyin, Hong Jingping, Jiang Yuren, Xu Jingfu, Yuan Xiluo, Sun Dongwen, Dong Xiujia, Wu Xiangfu, Du Ting _, Zhang Zhijiang (represented by Zhu Chang), Yang Xingqin, Ma Yuanfang, Cao Minghuan, Sun Bowen, Liu Bochang, Yu Xiaochuan, Wang Jingting, Gu Lunan (represented by Zhu Runzhi), Hu Jianchun, Cao Deliang (represented by Yu Xiaochuan), Wang Jingyu, Yang Weiyu, Liu Fuchen, Pan Mengqiao, Yang Hongshu, Pan Zhixing, Zhao Qingyi, Hong Lanxiang, Pang Shusen, Sha Yankai, Wang Kecheng, Cai Huan, Zhao Zhengping, Zhang Gongquan, Huang Boqiao (represented by Zhao Zhengping), Li Bochui, Wang Boquan, Xi Jiuru, Gu Junyi, Chen Yuren, Sun Jiyi, Chen Feishi, Qiu Laizhi (represented by Chen Feishi), Zhao Shuyong, Dong Shoujing, Zhao Zhujun (represented by Zhao Shuyong), Shen Mianhou, Zhu Shuyuan, Leng Yuqiu, Tang Shoumin, Wu Jichen (represented by Leng Yuqiu), Su Qiliu, Yang Mianzhai, Dong Mocha, Wang Lanqing, Wu Yanqiu, Yu Jingtang, Wang Haoru, Zhang Hongye, Jiang Jun, Lu Xiaobo, Gu Jingcheng, Wu Heting, Zhou Fohai, Ouyang Yanqing, Huang Lisan (represented by Ling Huian), He Yushu, Li Mingyang, Shu Shifu, Gu Zhutong, Zhao Qilu, Han Deqin, ninety-seven people in total, as well as representatives and guests, dozens of people, the meeting began at 3 p.m., led by Chairman Gu of the Provincial Government, performed the rituals, and reported on the process of organizing the relief association and the mission it undertakes. Jiang Wenyu moved a motion to mourn the martyrs of the anti-Japanese war and the compatriots who died in the war zone. All stood up and observed a three-minute silence.

▲ Speeches by the members. Then speeches were given by the members, all of which were solemn and tragic. The main points were nothing more than (1) reporting on the miserable conditions of the war zone, (2) that the areas of Jiangsu that were not war zones were affected by the war, with industry and commerce in a state of despair and in need of revitalization, so there was no surplus capacity to save others, (3) that financial stagnation in various counties was due to the concentration of cash in Shanghai, and Shanghai's financial hub had close ties with the central Ministry of Finance, so to seek relief for the war zone, the central government must first make it possible for non-war zones to have financial activity, (4) that it was the inherent duty of the people of Jiangsu to save Jiangsu, but the people of Songhu, Baojia, and Tai were sacrificing for the entire country, so relief should also be requested from the central government at the same time, (5) whether the Chinese nation could fight for survival depended on whether it could endure foreign disasters without being subdued, whether the pain that the Japanese gave our people could be reduced, and whether everything that the Japanese could destroy could be rebuilt to restore it. Today's meeting already has this kind of motivation. Whether it can be used to expand and enrich it, on the one hand, whether the government has political and moral responsibility, and on the other hand, whether the people have moral and national responsibility, (6) that relief for the war zone must first determine the four principles of scope, method, talent, and financial resources, (7) that the government and the people should cooperate and not go down two separate roads, and (8) that the people should demand from the government the "right to survival" and the "right to labor," and should not aimlessly seek unrealistic freedom and equality, because the disease of China lies in irregular excessive freedom and equality.

▲ The motion was organized, and Jiang Wenyu, Leng Yuqiu, Zhu Dexuan, Zhang Yipeng, Yang Weiyu, and Zhao Housheng were appointed as members of the motion organization committee. At 6 p.m., the photo was taken, and the ceremony was completed.

▲ Formal General Meeting. Starting on the morning of the 29th, the association held a formal meeting. In the morning, they discussed fundraising methods and generally decided to issue public bonds, borrow from banks, and request supplementary allocations from the central government. In the afternoon, they discussed relief and tax exemption cases, and elected standing committee members. Regarding fundraising methods, (1) one million yuan should be allocated first for emergency relief from military disasters, (2) a report should be submitted to the central government to issue 200,000 yuan in war zone relief bonds and allocate 5 million yuan in cash. Before the issuance, disaster relief bonds should be allocated and processed quickly, (3) another 5 million yuan should be raised from various banks for immediate use, and (4) another loan of American wheat should be obtained. Regarding representatives for overseas fundraising, those who are familiar with overseas Chinese must be competent, so they have not been recommended, and it is planned that the standing committee will appoint them. Borrowing from the banking sector for emergency needs will also be handled by the standing committee. Regarding the association's plan to issue military disaster bonds and request the central government to allocate cash, they must petition the Ministry of Finance for consultation and negotiation. Han Zishi, Leng Yuqiu, Zhang Yunbo, Jiang Wenyu, Lin Kanghou, Shi Liangcai, Chen Guangfu, and Zhang Gongquan were recommended to be responsible for this. Subsequently, the standing committee members were elected, including Shi Liangcai, Zhu Ziqiao, Zhu Yinjiang, Mu Ouchu, Tang Weizhi, Zhang Gongquan, Chen Guangfu, Zhang Zhongren, Han Zishi, Du Yuesheng, Ma Yuanfang, Gu Mosan, Zhao Cihua, Dong Dingsan, Shu Shiwen, Zhou Fohai, and He Menglin, seventeen people in total. The heads and deputy heads of each group were elected: General Affairs: Jiang Wenyu, Jin Baoguang, Yang Weiyu; Finance: Zhang Gongquan, Wu Yunbao, Shu Shiwen; Design: Zhao Housheng, He Yushu, Dong Xiujia; Relief: Huang Renzhi, Cheng Yiqing, Zhao Qilu; Statistics: Chen Guangfu, Leng Yuqiu, Han Deqin; Audit: Pan Xulun, Jin Houcheng. The standing committee of the Shanghai office of the association was elected as Zhu Ziqiao, Zhang Gongquan, and Shi Liangcai. If Zhu goes north, Chen Guangfu will be replaced. (April 30th)

◎ Local News 100

After interrogation, he also admitted without hesitation that he was spying on military intelligence for the enemy. His crime was heinous and deserved the death penalty. After the report was approved by the commander-in-chief Jiang's telegram, the prisoner was taken to the execution ground and executed by firing squad on the 1st.

▲ Recent Situation in Kunshan After Kunshan was harassed by enemy planes, the residents fled. Now that the military situation has gradually eased, most of them have returned. Pawnshops and businesses have already fully opened, but the business is deserted, while small vendors are making a lot of money. The farmers in the surrounding villages are carrying out their spring farming because our army is kind and approachable. Small steamers to Taicang, Liuhe, Jiaozhi, and other places have been operating normally since the 28th, and navigation in various villages is also unimpeded, just like normal. The reporter went to Tai on a steamer on the 28th to understand the situation in Taicang and saw that the shops in the city were also operating as usual, without any signs of war. It is heard that the farmers in Xiangqiao in the third district are begging for food from wealthy households because they have no food, which is very pitiful. On the way through Qingyang Port, they saw that our army's defense was solid and the morale was high, but in order to prevent spies from mixing in, the inspection was quite strict.

▲ Japanese Planes Fly Over Pinghu for Reconnaissance Pinghu Correspondence: Today (the 1st) at 9:40 a.m., a Japanese plane flew from the Jiashan area for low-altitude reconnaissance and circled the city. It happened to be the first day of the opening of the county's fifth sports meeting, and more than 10,000 people gathered on the field. They hurried to disperse to avoid danger.

▲ Restaurant Industry Appeals for Donation of Banquet Education Tax The Wuxi Banquet Education Tax was taken over by Qian Yinzai last September. All banquet taxes in the urban area were contracted by 27 restaurants as a whole, totaling 700 yuan per month, payable in three installments. Within the five months of the contract, they were still able to barely pay on time. However, since the start of the Shanghai war, the restaurant business has plummeted. Five restaurants, including Daxinlou, Daqinglou, Yongxinglou, Yuebinlou, and Xinjuxing, have closed down one after another, which has affected the tax revenue. Even those who have not closed down have not been able to pay the tax as before due to the slow business. Therefore, since this tax revenue is related to education funding, a special request has been submitted to the county government to strictly pursue the payment and order the restaurant guild to pay off the arrears in full within five days. The restaurant guild has written to the Chamber of Commerce to appeal and has repeatedly stated the difficulties, requesting the Chamber of Commerce to transfer the matter to the tax collection office and pay 20% of the contract amount from February 1st of this year, otherwise, they request that someone be sent to directly check the accounts and collect the tax in order to avoid losses and sympathize with the merchants' difficulties.

Jiangbei Bandit Xia Heshang Captured Nantong Correspondence: Xia Heshang, the famous bandit leader in Jiangbei Tongru counties, was captured after he escaped to Pingchao on the 30th, after assembling people and committing arson, robbery, and murder in multiple cases that had been wanted by the provincial and county governments without success. He was captured by the police and sent to the county government that night to be interrogated by the Pacification Military Law Office.

▲ Liang Guanying Thoroughly Investigates Extortion Case Nantong Correspondence: Liang Guanying, the commander-in-chief of the 25th Route Army, felt alarmed and dumbfounded by the case of extortion of huge sums of money under the guise of the army in Tongcheng. He ordered the Chief Inspectorate stationed in Tong to thoroughly investigate. The principal offender, Li Yezhong, is at large and has been wanted.

▲ Problems Still Exist for Opening of Money Industry Nantong Correspondence: The Nantong money industry has not yet resumed business, mainly because the accounts released cannot be recovered, and the transactions with various banks and villages in Shanghai have not been settled. The total amount owed by large and small firms is around 2.5 million yuan. Therefore, the settlement of accounts is the prerequisite for the current situation. As a result of the continuous meetings of the money industry, they will first start with the collection of money, and at the same time send representatives to negotiate with the financial circles in Shanghai and Zhenjiang to determine the date of listing.

▲ Murderer of Seventeen Lives Captured Gaoyou Correspondence: Bai Weixiang, the head of Gongtian Township in the second district of the county, was accused of killing seventeen civilians. The families of the deceased had successively sued the county government, and the county government questioned and detained Bai after three summons. Now, Jiang Changzhong, the family member of the deceased, unintentionally saw Bai Weixiang's eldest son Changxu, second son Changkun, and Zhang Mingzhi, the accomplice, at the Zhenjiang Railway Station. He immediately reported to the railway police, who arrested them and sent them to the Provincial Public Security Bureau for transfer to the local court for trial. ◎ A Casino is Openly Established in Zhabei Under the Japanese Power 104

▲ Publicly Printing and Distributing Leaflets to Attract Gamblers

▲ Saying the Protection is Comprehensive and the Hospitality is Thoughtful

Zhabei has been occupied by the Japanese army for several months now, and unscrupulous traitors such as Hu Lifu and Chang Yuqing are blatantly carrying out activities under the guise of violent protection. Yesterday, the reporter happened to visit a friend in a large hotel and suddenly found two strange cards. The paper was pink and brightly colored. One was about three inches long and two inches wide, and the other was the same length but one-third narrower. Both were printed with gold characters in the official script. After reviewing the full text, it was learned that it was a novel leaflet in the form of an advertisement for a large-scale casino newly established in the Japanese-occupied area. A special edition was attached, and the original text is recorded below to prove the bizarre phenomenon in Zhabei under the Japanese power. It is equipped with all kinds of gambling games, and the interior decoration is gorgeous. Protection is safe, tea, cigarettes, wine and water, the hospitality is thoughtful. Cars are provided for pick-up and drop-off. All circles of gentry and ladies are welcome to visit in their spare time. Sincerely, Dali Company Club." On the back, it is also printed with words such as "Note: Gambling games are welcome to visit." Another paper is printed with "The visiting address is No. 118 Derunli, Linping Road, at the end of Fair Road." When the Japanese see this, it is unknown how they will explain it.

▲ Only Three Provinces Remain Without Public Sales

▲ News of Central Government Public Sales as Well

The Republic of China Anti-Drug Association, due to the recent rush by various provinces to implement public opium sales, and the news that the central government is also considering restoring the public sales system, yesterday sent a letter to Wang Jingwei, President of the Executive Yuan of the National Government, requesting a clear announcement of the central government's opium prohibition policy, so that the public can understand the truth. The original letter is recorded below: "Extremely Urgent. Respectfully presented to Wang Jingwei, President of the Executive Yuan of the National Government in Luoyang. Our country is plagued by internal difficulties and disasters, and is subjected to external insults and plundering. Wounds have not healed, and collapse is still feared. However, the military and political authorities of various provinces, disregarding the imminent demise of the country, are still only seeking profit. They are relentlessly pursuing the opium public sales system, which will destroy the country and exterminate the race. Fujian and Anhui started it first, followed by Yunnan, Hubei, Hebei, Suiyuan, Chahar, and Rehe. The corruption is rampant, and the whole country is in a frenzy. Except for Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shandong provinces, which have not implemented public sales, all other provinces are gradually implementing it, helping each other in their chaos, disregarding the lives of the people, destroying the prohibition laws, and showing the utmost contempt. Yet the central government remains deaf and silent, without uttering a word, leading corrupt officials to become emboldened and opium addicts to become daring. They say that if it were not for the central government's indulgence and tolerance, this would not have happened. Rumors of the central government's brewing of opium public sales revival have been circulating for some time. At this time of national crisis and widespread anxiety, just when the central government is restoring corrupt policies, rumors are flying, seemingly not without cause. Public sentiment is wavering, and public opinion is boiling. The danger of collapse and disintegration is lurking everywhere. You, sir, are a revolutionary predecessor, a follower of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen, and hold a central position, from which government orders are issued. You should be building merits for the Party and the country, presiding over major plans, promoting benefits and eliminating evils. Furthermore, when the central government implemented public sales in the past, and mass organizations launched protests, you, sir, presided over the Guangdong government and were the first to express opposition. Your firm and upright spirit, I trust, is still strong. You will not have a protective heart towards this policy of indulging in poison. I dare to ask you, sir, to be open and honest, and announce the central government's opium prohibition policy and measures to stop the implementation of public sales in various provinces, so that the public can understand the truth, dispel doubts, comfort public opinion, and maintain national discipline. If you, sir, can make a prompt and decisive decision to strongly advocate for opium prohibition, assist the central government, and change policies, then this association and the entire nation will wholeheartedly support you and praise you endlessly. I await your orders with bated breath. The Republic of China Anti-Drug Association bows in respect. Jiang [seal]."

◎ Public Concession Crime Prevention Fund 107

In 1927 (the 16th year of the Republic), the number of criminal cases in Shanghai increased significantly. At that time, several Chinese individuals wrote to the Municipal Council, praising the efforts of the police officers and seeking ways to express their encouragement. Subsequently, the Chairman of the Municipal Council, the Chief of Police, and the Chief of Finance suggested initiating a fund, named the Special Fund for Crime Prevention. In January of the following year, the Municipal Council announced the start of collecting donations, which were entirely voluntary. Each donor was given a number, but their names were not publicized. The donations were used to hire special detectives, reward diligent police officers, reward informants, and provide compensation for those injured or killed. Thus, the Crime Prevention Fund was established. The details of its operation were scattered in the Municipal Gazette of December 1927 and January and February of the following year.

In March 1928, three Chinese individuals were publicly selected to serve as members of the Fund Committee. These three gentlemen have served continuously for four years and have held a total of sixteen meetings. All bonuses issued have been approved by the committee. In total, over 30,000 yuan in bonuses have been issued in the past four years. In addition, the committee has made other suggestions and contributions to the police department. The secretary of the committee is Mr. Ayers of the police department.

In May 1929, the Fund Committee first suggested adding motorcycles and increasing the number of police officers to combat robbers and kidnappings. Due to the large amount of money required, after much deliberation and discussion, in January 1931, the Municipal Council formulated a kidnapping prevention plan. The general outline was to establish telephones on the roads, purchase wireless police cars, add car and motorcycle teams, establish a special plainclothes police force, and set up a reserve team in the western district. This plan has been gradually implemented.

Since the establishment of the Fund Committee, within four years, a total of 547 bonuses have been issued, with 316 people receiving less than 50 yuan, 205 people receiving between 50 and 100 yuan, 17 people receiving between 100 and 200 yuan, and 5 people receiving between 200 and 350 yuan. In addition, compensation was given to the families of four police officers who died in the line of duty, each family receiving 500 yuan. The cases involved a total of 268 cases, including 36 armed kidnappings, 22 murders and attempted murders, 109 robberies and attempted robberies, 13 burglaries, 26 snatchings, 4 threatening letters, 27 illegal possession of firearms, 1 abduction, 16 thefts, 4 pickpocketing cases, and 10 other cases.

Among those who received bonuses and prizes were a 12-year-old boy who was a shop owner, a chauffeur, a garbage collector, a rickshaw puller, the wife of the victim, a bodyguard, a doorman, a shop assistant, a Russian shop assistant, a foreigner, a foreign soldier, and other upper-class people, as well as many informants. Some of those who did not accept money were given silver shields, silver cigarette cases, or couplets. From the variety of recipients, one can see the wide scope of the committee's work. In addition, the committee distributed tens of thousands of flyers and hired people to explain the key points of theft prevention to the public.

Since its establishment, this fund has received a total of 65,599.37 yuan in donations and 9,169.47 yuan in interest, totaling 74,768.84 yuan. In the past four years, a total of 30,490 yuan has been spent. As of the end of 1931, there was a remaining balance of 44,278.84 yuan.

◎ Women's Temperance Society Prepares to Hold Mother's Day 108

◎ Xiang Sheng Automobile Company Expands Business 109

Xiang Sheng Automobile Company was originally founded solely by Zhou Xiang Sheng, a Ningbo businessman in Shanghai. Since its establishment ten years ago, its business has been quite prosperous. Recently, considering the lack of a large-scale automobile company founded entirely by Chinese, he specially invited Ningbo gentlemen He Jingshan, Li Binchen, Yang Wenshou, Wang Zhengqu, and Zhou Zhiqing to join him, increasing the capital by 100,000 yuan and reorganizing it into a limited liability company. In addition to the existing 30 Buick automobiles, 50 new 1932 Chevrolet sedans were added. It is said that all the drivers have been re-trained and have reliable guarantors. The telephone number has been changed to 40000. The fare is one yuan for each pick up and drop off, regardless of distance, and three yuan per hour. He Jingshan was appointed chairman of the board, and Zhou Xiang Sheng was appointed general manager, in order to compete with a certain large company. Although the cars are not domestically produced, they do recover some of the profit rights. Fellow countrymen, please support them.

◎ Snatching a Wharf Almost Led to Disaster 111

The Nanyang Brothers Tobacco Factory in Hongkou employs many male and female workers. However, most of the workers reside in Pudong. Every day, they go out early and return late, and more than a thousand people travel back and forth on sampans and ferries from the Xiaonanyang wharf in Lujiazui, Pudong. As a result, there are also four or five hundred sampan and ferry boatmen who rely on this for their livelihood. For many years, they have lived in peace. However, recently, a local man named Yan Shaosheng coveted the rich income of the wharf and rented two small steam launches, intending to eliminate the sampan and ferry boats altogether. Yesterday morning, around four o'clock, he sailed the steam launches to the Lujiazui wharf and began operating. The sampan and ferry boatmen, fearing that their livelihoods would be taken away, gathered more than a hundred sampans and ferries, surrounded the steam launches, and, accompanied by their elders and children, questioned Yan face-to-face to protect the livelihoods of hundreds of people. Although there were police officers at the scene, they deeply understood the plight of the boatmen. After people tried their best to mediate, Yan realized that he had insufficient grounds and quickly ordered the steam launches to leave the wharf.

◎ Unruly Daughter-in-Law Convicted 114

▲ Sentenced to One Year and Two Months in Prison

A-liu, also known as Cui Bao, the youngest daughter of Ye Huang, an old local woman living in a bungalow at Kangjili, Kangti Road, in the French Concession, was scheduled to marry Chen Qiao, an accountant at the Mayer Silk Weaving Factory, on the 11th of last month. Ye Huang had prepared a dowry of thousands of yuan for her daughter, including clothing and jewelry. This aroused the jealousy of her eldest daughter-in-law, Ye Zhang, who resented her mother-in-law for spending so much money on her daughter's wedding. On the 7th of last month, Ye Zhang demanded 3,000 yuan from her mother-in-law but was unsuccessful. That night, at 10 o'clock, Zhang took advantage of her mother-in-law's sleep and sneaked into her room, biting her mother-in-law's lower body. Not satisfied, the next morning, she burned all of her sister-in-law's wedding clothes and took away the gold jewelry. The case was reported to the police station, and Detective Zhu Caicheng arrested Zhang and sent her to the Second Special District Court. The police station charged her with injuring a senior relative and destruction of property, based on Articles 293, 298, and 382 of the Criminal Code. The plaintiff also hired a lawyer to represent her and requested an incidental private prosecution to recover the destroyed clothing and stolen jewelry. The case was repeatedly heard by Wang Gangxu, the head of the criminal court, together with clerk Zhu Chengzhuo and prosecutor Wu Xiaoke. The defendant was defended by a lawyer. After the debate was concluded, the date for the verdict was set, as reported earlier. Yesterday was the day of the verdict. The plaintiff and her lawyer arrived at the court to await the announcement. At 10:00 AM, Judge Wang arrived at the criminal court and ordered the defendant to be brought to the court. After a brief interrogation, the verdict was announced: Ye Zhang was sentenced to one year and two months of imprisonment for injuring a senior relative. The number of days of detention before the judgment is final will be credited at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. The part of the incidental civil suit will be transferred to the civil court for trial. It is said that the defendant is still dissatisfied with the verdict and wants to file an appeal. The sensational case of intergenerational conflict has temporarily come to an end.

◎ Abusing a Maid by Tying Her Hands 115

▲ Arms and Legs Covered with Scars

▲ Owner Fined, Maid Sent to Charity

Yu Hu, a woman from Wuxi residing at No. 392 Xiamen Road, bought a 12-year-old Wuxi girl, Wu Baodi, as a maid last winter for 20 yuan. However, Yu Hu had a very violent temper and often beat her. The night before last, at 2:30 AM, she again beat Wu with a wooden stick for some reason. After Wu cried out for help, Mao Zhaolong, who lived in the same house, could not bear it and reported it to the Laozha Police Station. Chinese Detective Feng Xiushan was sent to investigate. He found Yu's door locked, and Wu was crying inside. He broke down the door and found the girl tied to the window frame. He untied her and arrested Yu at the nearby paint shop, bringing her and the rope and wooden stick to the police station. The police chief ordered her to be detained, and Wu was sent to the hospital. The doctor examined her and found scars on her arms, legs, and back, and issued a medical certificate. Yesterday morning, she was sent to the Criminal Court No. 1 of the First Special District Court. Police Lawyer Qian Xunjiu explained the case, and the maid, Wu Baodi, complained about the abuse, saying that she did not want to go back with her mistress and wanted to go to the Jiliang Institute to study. Defendant Yu Hu confessed that she often stole copper coins, so she had given her a slight beating, but claimed that the girl was bought as an adopted daughter, not as a slave. Without any debate from her lawyer, Judge Zhou Han examined the confession and ruled that Yu Hu was guilty of illegal imprisonment and injury, and fined her 80 yuan. Wu was sent to the Jiliang Institute to be cared for, and the rope and wooden stick were confiscated.

◎ Weather Report 122

The Xujiahui Observatory's meteorological forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the lower reaches of the Yangtze River would be cloudy and unsettled, with thunderstorms. The coastal area south of Shandong and Ma'an Island would be cloudy and foggy. The cyclone here and in the northern East China Sea is intensifying, due to a low-pressure area passing and moving towards the northeast-east. The winds are strong and erratic in the remaining coastal areas. The center of the hurricane was located at noon within 20 miles of the intersection of 10 degrees north latitude and 110 degrees east longitude, moving northwest. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in the city was 79.7 degrees at its highest and 65.8 degrees at its lowest. On the same day last year, the highest was 76.8 degrees and the lowest was 49.6 degrees.

Educational News

Important News 124

◎ Ministry of Education Order on Children's Memorial Day Measures

▲ To Be Included in Primary School Calendars Starting in Academic Year 21

The Ministry of Education has designated April 4th as Children's Memorial Day and has issued a special order to the consulates abroad, the education departments of various provinces and cities, and the Weihaiwei Management Office: "The Ministry has already formulated measures for the celebration of Children's Day, as ordered by the Executive Yuan, and issued them in Instruction No. 382 for compliance and reported them to the Executive Yuan for record. Starting from academic year 21, this day should be included in the primary school calendar to show solemnity and promote it. In addition to separate orders, it is hereby ordered that you comply and instruct your subordinates to comply with this order."

▲ Children's Memorial Day Measures

1. Purpose: The purpose of holding the memorial is to inspire children's interests, enlighten children's love of their country and family, and awaken society's attention to children's affairs.

2. Measures:

甲. Each primary school (kindergarten) should hold the following events:

子. Lecture on the anecdotes of revolutionary martyrs and great men of ancient China (focusing on highlighting the virtues of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, righteousness, faith, harmony, and peace) or the childhood lives of scientists and inventors from around the world.

丑. Performances that inspire children's love of their country and family (with special emphasis on parental love) through games or short dramas.

寅. Printing and distribution of colored picture cards on child education and hygiene.

卯. Giving out Children's Day souvenirs (such as stationery, pictures, and utensils, limited to students of the school or kindergarten).

辰. Parent-teacher conference for children of the school or kindergarten.

巳. Health competition or sports meet for children of the school or kindergarten.

午. Exhibition of literary and artistic achievements of children of the school.

In addition, various activities that arouse interest may be held, such as the election of model children, etc.

乙. Each social education institution (such as the public education center) should hold the following events:

子. Convene a Children's Day memorial meeting (encouraging local people to bring their children to participate) and hold a Children's Day memorial parade if deemed appropriate.

丑. Publicly exhibit various statistical charts on local children's surveys.

寅. Hold infant competitions and children's health or children's intelligence competitions, awarding prizes to the top few.

卯. Lectures on "The Responsibilities and Obligations of Parents," "Prenatal Care," "Childbirth Care," "Infant Care" common knowledge, "Methods of Training Wise Fathers and Good Mothers," and "The Necessity of Social Relief for Orphaned and Impoverished Children."

辰. Contact local child welfare organizations (such as nurseries and orphanages) and groups that seek the well-being of children to expand publicity on child welfare and child relief.

巳. Print and distribute pamphlets with common knowledge on "Child Hygiene," "Prenatal Care," and "Infant Care" and distribute them to parents.

午. Show films or dramas about children's lives and welcome children to visit.

未. Local art galleries, museums, etc. should be specially opened to children and welcome them to visit.

申. Encourage each family to hold the following events at home on this day:

(1) Family gatherings for children with relatives and friends.

(2) Celebrate the holiday: adults give gifts to children, and older children give gifts to younger children (gifts are limited to domestic goods, mainly those that can arouse children's love of beauty and have scientific meaning).

(3) Prepare glutinous rice snacks specially steamed for Children's Day (the design of these foods should have educational meaning) to add to the festive atmosphere.

酉. Encourage children to engage in the following appropriate games:

(1) Flying kites.

(2) Playing baseball.

(3) [Blank Space]

(4) Other.

◎Ministry of Education Issues Order to Compile Educational Yearbook 125

The Ministry of Education, in order to compile the Chinese Educational Yearbook, issued an order on the 2nd to the Education Departments of all provinces and cities, and to all universities, stating:

The Ministry is currently preparing to compile the first Chinese Educational Yearbook. It urgently needs to collect materials on important facts concerning education in our country, both past and present, in order to organize and compile them into a special volume. The content is divided into five sections: A. General Overview of Education, B. Educational Laws and Regulations, C. Overview of Education, D. Educational Statistics, E. Educational Miscellany. Each section is divided into chapters, and each chapter is divided into items. It is expected to be completed by August, reviewed and approved before October, and sent to print in November. However, the compilation of this book is a pioneering undertaking and relies on the collective wisdom and efforts of all to be successful. In addition to assigning special personnel to be responsible for handling it, various lists of reporting and submission items and formats for summary outline survey forms, etc., have been printed and distributed, ordering the presidents of the schools to appoint special personnel to accurately fill in the forms and submit them by June 30th. However,宁缺毋滥 (better to have none than have inferior ones), standards should be strict, save space, and the writing should be concise. The compiler can sign their name for commemoration. (23) Compile and submit an overview of all public and private (private ones are limited to those that have been approved or registered) colleges and above that have been closed in each province and city (Explanation 1). (Explanation 1) Items marked with "2" require two copies, one to be filled out by the Provincial and Municipal Education Bureaus, and one by the Counties and Cities. Items marked with "1" require one copy, to be filled out by the Provincial and Municipal Education Bureaus. (Explanation 2) For items not marked with "1" or "2", there are no specific requirements, and the Provincial and Municipal Education Bureaus should fill them out based on the facts. (Explanation 3) Reporting items for the Provincial and Municipal Education Bureaus should be submitted by June 30th. The deadline for reporting items for the Counties and Cities should be extended to July 31st. B. List of Items to be Submitted by Education Departments of Provinces and Cities: (1) Individual educational laws and regulations of each province and city. If they have not been printed, important laws and regulations concerning educational administration, school education, and social education should be selected and submitted in full. (2) Proceedings of educational conferences in each province and city over the years, such as the proceedings of principals' conferences and directors' conferences. (3) Publications recording educational exhibitions in each province and city over the years. (4) Publications recording sports meets in each province and city over the years. C. Key points of the overview of studying abroad. D. Key points of the overview of academic institutions and academic organizations. E. Key points of the overview of universities and colleges.

◎Statistics of Chinese Students at the Sino-French University in Lyon 126

◎Meeting of Destroyed Middle Schools Scheduled 127

▲Tomorrow at 10:00 AM

Since the outbreak of the Sino-Japanese War, several middle schools in the war zone, such as Guangzhong, Shibei, Lida, Chizhi, Aiguo, Nanyang Commercial High School, and China Women's Physical Education College, have been burned down, resulting in significant losses. It is now reported that these schools have scheduled a joint meeting at 10:00 AM on May 5th (Thursday) at Nanyang Commercial High School in Weifengli, west of the intersection of Weihaiwei Road and Tongfu Road, to discuss remedial measures after the disaster. However, it is feared that the number of secondary schools affected by the disaster is more than just these few, so all affected secondary schools can send one representative to attend at that time.

◎Relief Society Opens Temporary School for Child Refugees 128

The temporary relief society for refugees in the war zone of this city, considering that many of the refugees are children who have lost their schooling, which is very regrettable, has formulated a temporary education plan. The society's first boarding house has been opened since the eighth of last month, with about seventy or eighty students. Two large classrooms have been set up in the Qīngliáng Temple location of the boarding house, divided into Class A and Class B, and taught by staff members of the boarding house in groups. Classes have been held for three weeks now, and it is reported that the results are good.

Jinan University Library Safe and Sound 129

Due to its geographical location, Jinan University in this city has been under serious threat from Japanese air forces. It has already been relocated to Shanghai, Suzhou, and Guangzhou to continue classes as usual. The university's library, with its large collection of Chinese and Western books, was evacuated to Shanghai after the January 28th Incident [1932]. Except for some newspapers and unbound magazines, there were no losses. A Western-style house on Xinzha Road has been rented as a place to store the books. It has been organized and opened for reading, and everything has been restored to its former state. On average, about a hundred people read there day and night. The library has tens of thousands of volumes, which have been preserved safely.

Sports

◎Large-Scale North China Games Venue 130

-A Glimpse of Various Architectural Designs-

(Kaifeng Correspondence) The 16th North China Games will be held in Kaifeng this autumn. Although it is a time of national crisis, construction is still actively underway. The venue is large-scale and has everything that is needed, including a running track, long jump pits, changing rooms for male and female athletes, a football field, a tennis court, a volleyball and basketball court, a grandstand, a spectator stand, fences, a swimming pool, staff rooms, a gym, offices, a children's playground, a skating rink, and a horticultural area, covering a very large area. The organizing committee has also compiled and printed "Explanation of Detailed Drawings of the Sports Venue," which is now published and details the plans for various constructions at the venue. Excerpts are as follows:

▲The straight length of the running track is 220 meters, the circumference is 400 meters, the width of the straight length is 12 meters, which can be divided into 12 lanes. The width of the circumference is 8 meters, which can be divided into 8 lanes for running 400 meters and 400-meter hurdles. The distance between the outer perimeter of the running track and the grandstand is 4 meters, with a fence in between.

▲The long jump pit, high jump pit, pole vault pit, and long jump pit should be separated because the North China Games are divided into high school, middle school, and women's divisions and must be held simultaneously in different parts and items.

▲The size of the football field is stipulated to be 50 to 100 yards wide and 100 to 130 yards long. The boundary of this field is 80 meters wide (equivalent to 88 yards) and 110 meters long (equivalent to 120 yards). The distance between the field and the grandstand is 10 meters. The north is 6 meters from the fence and the south is 10 meters from the wire mesh. It can also be used as a baseball field and a softball field.

▲Tennis Court Tennis competitions are divided into singles and doubles. Each unit can have two groups of singles players and one group of doubles players competing at the same time. Therefore, there must be at least six tennis courts. This court is built according to the legally prescribed size, 36 feet wide and 78 feet long. The distance between the two courts is 4 meters. The distance between the side of the court and the grandstand is 7 meters. The distance between both ends of the court and the wire mesh is 6.5 meters.

▲Basketball and Volleyball Courts There are three basketball courts, each 15 meters (50 feet) wide and 28.60 meters (94 feet) long. The distance between the two courts is 5 meters. The distance between both ends and the wire mesh and fence is also 5 meters. The distance between the side of the court and the grandstand is 6.5 meters. There are two volleyball courts, each 11 meters wide and 22 meters long. The distance between the two courts and the basketball court is 5 meters. The distance between the court and the grandstand is 6.5 meters. One end is 6 meters from the wire mesh, and the other end is 10 meters from the sample pole. According to the North China volleyball competition, it is divided into high school, middle school, and women's divisions, and the size of the field is also different. The maximum dimension is the predetermined number. If the three divisions compete at the same time, the two courts will definitely not be enough. If necessary at the time, the basketball court can be temporarily converted into a volleyball court. (To be continued)

Gold Standard Soars Alarmingly 131

▲Another Increase of 8 Taels and 2 Mace

▲Buying Frenzy, Shorts Painfully Cover Yesterday, the gold market was only open for half a day, but the rise of the gold standard was even more severe, with a rapid trend. Heavy Pressure on Yarn and Cotton Market 136

Since the Shanghai Incident, all industries have been greatly affected. The yarn and cloth exchange was closed for three months and has now officially reopened the day before yesterday. Before the bidding for standard yarn began, it was widely expected that the price would be around 160 taels because the new standard was changed to 20 counts, raised by one grade. Unexpectedly, American cotton has recently experienced a sharp drop, putting even greater pressure. In addition, actual sales have been sluggish, and all parties are lifeless. Financial resources are drying up, and the situation in the interior is weakening, resulting in weak purchasing power from all sides. As a result, the yarn inventories of factories in Shanghai are gradually increasing, and Japanese factories have resumed operations and are working hard on production. Domestic yarn also has many strong competitors. According to market records for April, the total cotton yarn purchased by various groups was only over 10,000 bales. Due to all these reasons, the market unanimously views prices as low. The opening price of new standard yarn this month was only 155 taels and 3 mace, about 2 taels higher than the old standard price before January 28. Now, due to weak actual demand and a bad overall environment, the price has fallen by 1 tael this month alone.

▲ Standard Yarn Selling Pressure Rises: The market atmosphere for new standard yarn at the exchange was flat at the opening. Very few transactions took place in the market. Near-term prices fell by 2 mace over the past two months, while far-term prices rose by 2 mace. In the afternoon, due to excessive inventory this month, selling pressure was strong, with near-term prices falling by 1 tael and 2 mace, and far-term prices falling by 7 or 8 mace. The total trading volume for the day was only 6,600 bales, compared to 23,600 bales the previous day. It was found that 600 bales were sold by Taixing, 400 bales by Yiyu, 850 bales by Guangfeng, and 350 bales by Renfeng. 350 bales were purchased by Ruidai, 450 bales by Changfeng, and 250 bales by Xiesheng. Silk and Tea: Spring Silkworms in Yuhang Undergo Another Change

▲ Sudden Cold and Heat: Silkworms Discovered

In places like Pingyao and Jinjianong in Yuhang, this year's spring silkworms are mostly of foreign breeds, and the amount raised is only 40% of previous years. During the third sleep, there were several days of rain and cold weather, and diseases such as yellowing were discovered. Currently, the early silkworms have entered their major sleep. Unfortunately, in the past two days, although the weather has been sunny and warm, the weather has been hot and humid, and the silkworms have stopped feeding and are dormant, resembling silkworm plague. The spread is very rapid, and many have been discarded. This year's silkworm harvest is once again disappointing.

Qimen Tea Prices Soar 141

The official weighing of new Qimen black tea has been underway for several days. Prices in the southwest region remain above 100 yuan, while prices in Fuliang are also hovering around 80 yuan. Qingpianye (青片叶) tea leaves are opening at 1.4 yuan per catty, with the cost of producing dry tea reaching approximately 320 yuan per dan (approximately 7 catties). Bai Hao (白毫, white down) tea is opening at 800 wen per liang, making the cost even greater than that of Qingpian (青片). Qimen tea prices have reached their peak. The initial intention of various firms was to lower mountain prices to reduce costs, but the situation has changed dramatically with the arrival of new tea. The quality of the mountain tea produced by mountain households is excellent, and firms have not reduced prices. They insist on raising mountain prices, and fellow merchants are eager to start business early and cannot wait. They have no choice but to open pricing according to the market. Prudent firms know that costs are too high and that they will face danger. However, due to the market trend, any hesitation will lead to lost opportunities, so they have no choice but to join the frenzy. In the past two days, the weather has suddenly turned cool, and tea buds have slowed down their growth. Mountain households are leisurely picking and drying, and shipments are not surging, making it difficult to expect prices to fall.

Fuliang Mao Feng Already Has New Produce 142

The Qing tea from Dongshang Township in Fuliang County is experiencing a slow budding process this year due to the frequent cold weather. Recently, the weather has cleared up and turned warm, making it the perfect time to pick the first flush of Mao Feng tea. Therefore, mountain households are selecting the slightly longer tea buds and picking and processing them early, resulting in tender leaves and a rich aroma. New Mao Feng from areas such as Siqian, Shiding, and Yaoli has already appeared on the market, with prices ranging from 6 jiao to 7.5 jiao per catty. However, shipments are limited, and only Jingdezhen merchants have purchased small quantities, with no large transactions completed.

Sugar Market: Slight Increase in Coarse Sand and White Refined Sugar

Yesterday's trading at the Sugar Market Association was active, and the trend was firm. The trading price for Dutch sugar No. 24 coarse sand white was 12 taels, 8 qian, and 2.5 fen. Shipments from Xiamen were 12 taels and 7 qian, with the market shape still pretty. Taikoo Sugar B mark was called up to 16 taels and 3 qian, but few buyers accepted. DX mark was 15 taels and 2 qian and 5 fen, and HM mark was 13 taels and 7 qian, with slight transactions. The atmosphere was stable and graceful. Brokerage prices remained quiet. Taiyuan Ice Sugar recently continued to arrive, with brokers calling the original price of 9 taels and 8 qian. Due to sluggish sales, inquiries were very quiet.

Slight Rise in 9-Pound Coarse Cloth

▲ The trend of falling factory cloth has ceased, and actual sales are slightly more active. This is because the situation has progressed slightly, and there are rumors of the Jinghu (Beijing-Shanghai) Railway reopening, calming market sentiment. Yesterday, lightweight cloth turned to an increasingly firm trend, with 9-pound cloth rising by 2.5 fen. Jubaopen (聚寳盆), Sanji (三鷄), all at 4 taels, 1 qian and 7.5 fen. However, Maoying (猫英) 3 qian was willing to be sold off. Thirteen-pound cloth was slightly softer, with Jiutian (九天), Rendingqiu (人顶球), and Feixiong (飞熊) all at 5 taels and 5 qian. Sales of sixteen-pound cloth to the northern market were slightly active. Shuangyu (双鱼) Jiqing (吉庆) at 7 taels and 6 qian, Hongfu (鸿福) at 7 taels and 7 qian, Shuanglong (双龙) Sanxing (三星) at 7 taels and 8 qian. Due to the clandestine activity of Japanese factory goods recently, sales of fine cloth and fine twill have been quieter. Customer sales of dyed Yin Dan Qi Lin (阴丹七林) and Haichang Lan (海昌蓝), etc., have also been affected.

▲ The West Pi Tou (疋頭, piece goods) market is quiet, and all routes have depleted funds. In addition, there have been relatively many arrivals this year, so it is still difficult to turn the situation around. Yesterday, white-stripped Ma Sha (麻紗, linen yarn) Meizui (美最时) and Hekang (和康) brands had fallen to 2 qian and 7.5 fen. Zhuluomiao (珠羅秒) and Sheng Luo (生罗) and other products are typically in demand, but there is also no vitality. Yuan Yu Chou (元羽绸) and Taixi Duan (泰西缎) are not suited to the season, and there is even less opportunity. However, Piao Bu (漂布, bleached cloth) and Su Yang Miao (素洋秒) have slight, scattered sales.

Copper, Lead: Strong Momentum in the Tea Industry

As the new tea season approaches, the demand for copper and lead from the tea industry is increasing, making the market lively. In recent days, the market has seen a total of 1,500 dan of goods opened, and prices have increased by 1 qian due to the inconsistent supply of old and new goods on the market, selling for 13 taels and 9 qian per dan. However, market sentiment is very good, and there are also those who want 14 taels and 2 qian and 5 fen.
