Shen Bao (申報) Local Supplement, Wednesday, May 4, Year 21 of the Republic of China (No Additional Cost)

· Commentary

A Letter from Compound Gentleman 143

— Buddha

Since the outbreak of the war, this publication has been greatly affected and had to be temporarily suspended. Although it has recently resumed, the contributors are very different. For example, in the literary and art section, since the publication of the excellent works of Mr. Chen Zhu, Zun Meng, and Shaochang, there have been very few submissions of new poetry, while there have been many submissions and responses of old poetry. I see that the readers welcome this, so I include the old poetry. Benevolent people see benevolence, and wise people see wisdom. Since readers each have their own preferences, the editor has no need to interfere.

However, there is one point that I would like to discuss with Gentleman Fang and all the readers: Is poetry better when it is old, or is it better when it is new? Is it better when it has rhyme and melody, or is it better when it is unrhymed and just sung casually? This question has been debated fiercely by many literary giants at home, but there is still no concrete solution. However, my opinion is that writing is definitely more convenient when it is new - but I cannot say that it is better. If we are talking about what is better, new poetry has its advantages, and old poetry also has its advantages. However, I believe that poetry is better when it is old because since it is literature and art, it should naturally have some artistic quality, and it is definitely not something that can be considered poetry if it is just sung casually.

If you say that classicism does not conform to modern trends, in fact, classicism - not only now - has never conformed to trends. The so-called poetry of Li Bai and Du Fu can be understood by old women. If this is classicism, then how can old women understand it? Even Tang Jingchuan of the Ming Dynasty and Yuan Zicai of the Qing Dynasty mostly advocated natural learning and used less classicism. However, due to the convenience of writing and the elegance of art, they occasionally used it, but this cannot be called classicism. If you say that we only care about the masses and do not care about art, then why should this publication have a literary and art section? In general, people often have places where they cannot act directly, and writing also has such a difficulty. Although I have not met you, (here I originally wanted to use the phrase "knowing Jing," but I was afraid that you would scold me for using classicism to force it in, so I dare not,) but judging from the wording of your letter and your actions, you must be a young man who has not yet undergone a baptism in social situations and academic aspects.

As for science, to be honest, our country is indeed the poorest and most immature in this field compared to other countries. At the moment, we are still in the era of selling scientific knowledge. However, since there is a lot of selling, there will naturally be creators emerging. Now, our country's bread problem is causing a big panic. It is not easy to build big projects, so this publication's position is to promote general small crafts and small sciences, hoping that all the items needed in life will be entirely made domestically. As for ships, railways, airplanes, bombs, etc., government officials will naturally think of ways to do this, and we can ignore them. It is only because of this war that the tragedies in places like Wusong and Zhabei were all caused by the enemy's cannons, airplanes, and bombs. Therefore, recently, this publication has often published such similar sciences, only because the people of our country have suffered this kind of pain and are still clueless. Therefore, we publish them so that everyone knows the structure of airplanes and how powerful bombs are. I believe that although the masses cannot manufacture this kind of timely science, it is not impossible for the masses to know something about it, and it cannot be said that it is too far from the masses and has absolutely no value for publication.

Looking back, I also have to say a word to several contributing scientists. In the future, if you give us manuscripts, please do not send manuscripts of the type "What is water? What is aroma?" Please send what the raw materials of that thing are, whether it is made of salt or rosin or protein, and what kind of procedures and methods are used to make that thing. If you send such manuscripts, this publication will be even more welcome because it is quite in line with this publication's purpose of promoting small crafts.

Alas, editing this publication is really difficult. The first thing is that the space is narrow and cannot be fully published. The second thing is to match the tastes of the readers. As the saying goes, "The father-in-law wants wontons, and the mother-in-law wants noodles." Matching the tastes of the father-in-law does not match the tastes of the mother-in-law. How can we make the tastes of the newspaper-reading gentlemen in society mostly correct? I thought of an old story in foreign textbooks about a father and son both leading a donkey, which resulted in the donkey dying in the river. It can be seen that nothing in the world can please everyone. However, I will do my best to make my heart at peace.

In addition, I would like to inform the comrades who contribute manuscripts that the manuscripts should be as short as possible, and at most should not exceed 500 characters. If they are not used, they will not be returned. Because there are dozens of manuscripts submitted every day, the procedures are quite troublesome, and there are other difficulties. I will explain them later.

Literature and Art

Feeling the Times 144

— Mengshaozhu

Throwing heads to eliminate the bandit leaders,

Brave martyrs shake the remaining barbarians.

Ravenously drinking three feet of blade,

Pig returns empty, a carload of ghosts.

The world admires fame like Guo Jie,

Smiling Zhuan Zhu sets seven in the oven.

East wind cannot compete from now on,

For everything, ask emptiness' calculations.

Doggerel Verse - Dean Yong Shui Xing - Ti Ya 145

Language is pleasing, appearance is astonishing,

Spontaneous innocence is most endearing.

Alas, Yang Hua has a watery nature,

A thousand gold is not spared to marry a hooligan.

A beauty has been called city-overturning since ancient times,

A beauty passes by during national crisis.

Fifty is still like a virgin,

Her previous life must have been a demon.

Overthrow dictatorship, sing of double tribunals,

Day and night, seeking the leftists nearby.

After all, scholars lose to merchants,

The backstage is changed, not the front.

Obsessed with power, it is truly pitiful,

How can scholars lack the talent to govern?

If he had died a year earlier,

Who would not send wreaths?

Science

Newly Invented Safety Airplane 146

— Liu Qi

Although people who fly on airplanes now feel that traveling is fast, they are always apprehensive about the possibility of an airplane accident. If they fall to the ground, their lives will be in danger. Therefore, it is not easy for aviation to develop. This security issue is also very important. According to Reuters, a French engineer named Albert Sauvant has invented a safety steel box installed in airplanes to avoid danger. He conducted a field test on the 26th of last month, intentionally crashing his airplane into the cliff rocks beside the mountain at a height of 500 feet. The airplane spun six somersaults and crashed into pieces on the ground. At that time, Albert climbed out of the airplane and showed the frightened audience that the safety steel box in the airplane was not damaged at all.

This time, his test was not approved by the French authorities and was done privately. Now, he is requesting permission to test it again at a height of 3,000 feet. He has previously used model airplanes to test drops several times. The airplanes carried small lamb heads and some eggs. Because of the protection of the safety steel box, they were not damaged when they fell. In the future, if all airplanes are equipped with this kind of safety steel box, then air travel will not only be fast but also safe.

Unreasonable

National Crisis Period 147

— Zhang Luo

One afternoon, Mr. C met his friend Mr. Z on the road.

"Old Z, how have you been these days? Do you feel depressed?"

"Depressed! How can I not be depressed? I can't think of anything!"

" ... Want to stroll around the playground? What about the cinema? Dance hall? ... "

"No! I haven't been to any of them! What time is it now? A national crisis is upon us! How can I have the heart to have fun!" Mr. Z said sternly to Mr. C, expressing his extreme concern for the country.

"Ha! People's hearts are already dead! Chinese people are not willing to fight for respect! 'Five minutes of heat'! It has long been laughed at by others! What 'national crisis' or not, Chinese people are only fit to be 'slaves'! Haha! Old Z, what does it matter to have fun?"

Three days later, at the entrance of an XXX cinema, Mr. C saw his friend Mr. Z again ... The movie had just ended.

"Yo! Old Z, where are you going?"

" ... " Mr. Z was stunned, a little ashamed on his face!

"You were ... " Mr. C was very surprised.

"Watching a movie!" Mr. Z tried to pretend to be casual ... "Today's movie is very good!"

"Huh? Didn't you once say ... "

"Yes! During a national crisis! We shouldn't be having fun! But, look at the scene in Shanghai, does it still look like 'a national crisis period'? The 'five minutes of heat' has already passed! The image in my mind has gradually faded! Naturally, why should I try to fight for respect alone? Even if I do, it's useless, ha, ha, it's better for everyone to go for a stroll! Relax!"

"Hahaha! ... "

"Mr. C, let's go to XXX Western Restaurant together! Then we can go to the dance hall! I'll treat! ... "

" ... ... ... ... ... ... "

Among the many people in front of the cinema; at some point, the shadows of the two of them had disappeared.

Exposing the Magic Lantern

Proposing Marriage or Compiling Photos? 148

— Jin Huan

"A son of a certain aristocratic family, a graduate of high school, is currently employed in a certain institution and earns a considerable monthly income. Now, with the consent of his parents, he is widely seeking marriage. He hereby publishes in the newspapers to solicit lovers. Any willing lady, please attach a recent photo and a detailed resume and send it to Box No. X of this newspaper."

The above advertisement was published in a certain newspaper half a month ago. This was not a big deal, but it caught the attention of a certain lady who rarely reads newspapers.

She is currently working as an elementary school teacher, and she feels that her youth is about to fade away, so she is very anxious to find her partner. Usually, because her conditions are too harsh, it has been delayed year after year, and there is still no suitable person. Now, seeing such an advertisement, how can she not think that "the opportunity will not come again"? Therefore, she secretly sent her photo and resume, and also attached a few affectionate and eager words.

On the afternoon of the third day, she received a letter with a postage stamp attached, typed on a government machine. The letter said:

"Upon receiving your fragrant letter, I was overjoyed. However, I am mainly concerned about health in this marriage solicitation. Your graceful appearance is very much in line with my conditions, but the facial expression is not enough to represent the health of the whole body. Therefore, I am writing to you to respectfully request that you send me special poses of your chest, abdomen, legs, etc. within a week (please sign formally after the photos to prevent counterfeiting), so that we can grow old together and have no regrets forever. I think you will also express sympathy (the rest is omitted)."

Health? That is in line with my tastes. I remember that she also participated in the city sports meet last year. Although she was not as good as XXX, she also surpassed many female athletes. Now he really wants a "healthy and beautiful" woman. Perhaps she still has a hope of being selected. She was very pleased and unhesitatingly took many photos like the ones at the swimming pool, placed them in a brocade box, and sent them solemnly.

She thought about it all day long, she thought about it all day long, the more she thought about it, the more she fantasized. She said with confidence that this matter would definitely succeed, and she would definitely not be rejected. Moreover, she also fantasized about the other person's physique. Perhaps he was also an athlete. Then, in the gym and swimming pool, it would be even more fun. She was so lost in thought that she almost went crazy.

Ah! Did Hong Qiao make a mistake? Why is it almost a week and she has not received his reply? She couldn't wait, so she wrote letters to ask. However, no matter how many letters she sent out, there were still no replies from the other side. She was annoyed, so she wrote to question him again. Sure enough, it came:

"Your instructions and photos have arrived. I have now obtained the consent of Ms. X and will be engaged immediately. I am sorry for your kind intentions and cannot help but apologize."

She was so angry that she couldn't speak after reading this short note.

"Proposing marriage or compiling photos?"

Became her last question;

Random talk

Debates Among Female Students 149

— ·蓓蕾·

The spring rain was gently pattering against the window, the air pressure felt heavy and dull. In the dormitory of XX Girls' School, the lights were already out. Most of the girls were seeking sweet dreams in their warm beds. However, the spring rainy night filled the hearts of the girls with emptiness and unease. Bored, they started a casual conversation again.

Female students, especially those in high school, often while away the long nights with aimless chatter. Yet, within this aimless chatter, there often exists a mysterious undercurrent.

In this dormitory, close to the school gardens, even with the rain, the fragrance of flowers faintly wafted through the air. Miss Qian's bed was next to the window. The fine rain falling on the leaves prevented her from falling asleep. So, she spoke first, calling to Xuan on the opposite bed:

"Hey, are you asleep yet? Tell us again about your experience escaping during the invasion and seeing people being abducted by enemy soldiers." Xuan, who was at this moment still haunted by the painful history of her escape, was not yet asleep. She replied to Miss Qian with a tone of shame and anger, "Such humiliating acts are difficult to describe. In short, we defenseless women are powerless to resist."

"Well, how did you manage to escape then?"

"Don't mention it, it's too embarrassing."

Ping and Ying, meanwhile, were quietly discussing whose lover was this way and whose fiancé was that way... The four people in the room had formed two pairs, each engaged in their own conversation.

Hearing Ying happily engaging in the same corrupt discussions as before, Xuan recalled how passionately Ying had given speeches everywhere before the Battle of Shanghai began. She couldn't help but taste her own ordeal and the contradiction it revealed. So, she called out to Ying, saying in a scolding tone, "Did the spirit of bravery dissipate with the sound of gunfire? Didn't you used to say that heroes who kill enemies could even demand kisses? Now that heroes have indeed emerged, are kisses being realized in practice? How can you be so passive after losing our territory!"

Ying, who was usually known for her debating skills, could not accept such words. She immediately retorted, "Am I passive? Am I afraid? People who aren't afraid wouldn't be in such a mess when they see enemy soldiers. What's all this talk about passive and active?"

These words seemed to pour fuel on Xuan's fire, who said, "We couldn't fight the enemy because we didn't have guns. I know that there are no sacrifices that are not in vain, and those who have value. At least, I personally experienced national calamity, which is better than you who only know how to talk empty words."

"I only know how to talk empty words? Yes, I wonder if those who speak the truth have ever realized anything?"

"That's just quibbling, it doesn't make any logical sense."

The two sides argued until they reached a boiling point. Ping and Miss Qian remained neutral, neither speaking nor mediating. Miss Qian was friendlier with Xuan, while Ping leaned toward Ying.

Just as the argument was getting heated, there were three gentle taps on the glass window. "No talking after lights out!" It was clearly the voice of the dormitory supervisor.

Thus, a debate that was unconsciously conscious came to an end. Only the gentle rain continued to patter against the flower branches.

Movie

The Tearful History of Youlan 150

—

"The Tearful History of Youlan," which premiered yesterday at the Nanjing Grand Theatre, is an unprecedentedly tragic and beautiful epic film. The protagonist, Elizabeth Landi, whose expressions in "Spiritual and Carnal Love" and "Yellow Permit" were well-appreciated by audiences, needs no further introduction. In this film, she plays a young woman whose husband falls in love with another. She laments her ill fate, but to protect her husband, she spares no effort to save him, even at the cost of throwing herself into danger and ending up in prison. Her due date arrives, and her newborn child is taken away. The separation of mother and child is extremely heartbreaking. Although she exhausts every possible means to retrieve her child, she is imprisoned again for kidnapping. Elizabeth Landi's performance is even more profound than in her previous films. Every movement and expression deeply moves the audience. The supporting actor, Mike Lauren, gives an outstanding performance. The rest of the cast also put in extraordinary effort, making this film a worthwhile watch.

Special Articles

Ford Small Car　Yu· 154

▲ Made in England

In the British automobile industry, a type of small car has recently become popular, known as the "baby" car. This type of small car is not only smaller in appearance than ordinary cars, but its engine horsepower is also reduced accordingly. In Britain, automobile taxes are calculated annually based on the horsepower of the car. Therefore, in recent years, most car drivers have been moving from large to small cars for economic reasons. Moreover, "baby" cars are not only cheaper to tax, but all driving expenses are also related to the smaller engine and reduced horsepower, which reduces the burden on car owners. In addition, there is another reason for purchasing a car, which is that its selling price is lower than that of ordinary cars. For this reason, small cars in Britain are very popular, and all automobile manufacturers are working hard to develop small cars. As a result, the display of "baby" cars occupies a large part of the automobile exhibitions held in England.

Ford cars have always had an advantage in sales in England. Ford has a branch in England, and its products are numerous, competing with British goods for a share of the market. Recently, in order to develop its business and keep up with the trend, Ford has created a small Ford car in England. According to news from London, this small car has eight horsepower, is beautifully styled, and is economical to use. It can compete with the current popular good small cars. It is expected that when this car is launched, there will be another boom in the British automobile industry.

The first model of the "baby" Ford car was manufactured in the United States and was completely designed and assembled manually. When it crossed the Atlantic Ocean to England, it was kept absolutely secret. This car was displayed at the Albert Hall in London on February 19, beginning its first meeting with the British people.

The new car's engine has four cylinders, with a size of 2.23 inches by 6.64 inches. It can generate 7.96 horsepower. According to this horsepower, the annual tax is 8 pounds. The cylinder head can be separated and is of integral construction. The lower half is cast together with the crankshaft box. The valves are made of high-quality alloy steel. Other engine components are also carefully refined. The car's wheelbase is seven feet six inches, and the track is three feet eight inches.

Regarding the price of this Ford small car, the cost calculation cannot be hastily calculated in the short term. Therefore, on the morning when the new car was displayed for public viewing, the selling price of the car could not yet be announced. The final official selling price will be announced later. A two-door sedan will be sold for 120 British pounds. In addition, a four-door sedan will also be launched soon.

The Ford small car is extremely well-made, and the spaciousness of the car body is also one of its characteristics. The rear seat position of this car is very comfortable, especially the rear compartment. Sitting in it, the legs feel very comfortable, without the discomfort of shifting and fidgeting. The headroom is even more spacious. Even a six-foot-tall person can sit upright with a hat on, without feeling uncomfortable at all. Therefore, getting in and out of the car is quick and easy, and the driver feels comfortable on both sides. Other equipment is naturally simplified due to the low and small body. However, there is still a fuel gauge. The position of the gear lever is quite appropriate. The position of the handbrake is a bit far, but in practice, it is only used for parking.

The car's generator is installed between the engine and the frame, in a very low position, which is not easy to touch. However, the location of the coil plug and distributor is convenient. Therefore, the appearance is also good. All of the above are the general details of this new small car. Ford's launch of a small car is a major change in its car-making history. The style of the small car is an English style, so its significance is even more important. The first car Ford made was the Model A with 24 horsepower. The second was a smaller one with 14.9 horsepower. Since then, there have been many changes, striving to meet the requirements of the times. Recently, the launch of small cars is due to economic reasons. However, Ford is still working hard to produce large cars. As for the future sales of this 8-horsepower small car, it is difficult to say for sure at this time. However, judging from its exquisite workmanship, low selling price, and the needs of the public, it should not be difficult to sell well and become popular.

A Stunning Achievement: The MG Midget · 155

Mr. Aston has already gained a fine reputation. On February 16th of last year, Mr. Aston drove a British car with an engine of less than 750cc and achieved a speed of 103.13 miles per hour over a five-kilometer course. Later, he drove ten miles and maintained a speed of over 100 miles per hour, achieving an average speed of 101.86 miles per hour, breaking the previous record. It is worth noting that Mr. Aston is the first person to achieve a speed of over 100 miles per hour with an engine of less than 750cc. The car he drove was an MG Midget. Those engaged in the construction of so-called small cars have long hoped that their products would achieve such results. However, only MG cars have succeeded in this endeavor. Although future advancements in automobiles are unlimited, MG's achievement is already commendable and worthy of praise. On October 17th of last year, Mr. Eyston again drove a 750cc MG car and achieved a speed of 110.28 miles per hour over a five-kilometer course. This is equivalent to the speed of Mr. Campbell in the Blue Bird II.

The history of the MG Car Company is particularly interesting. With personal enthusiasm and perseverance, coupled with the support and sympathy of the general manager, the company has made rapid progress and achieved its current position. Just seven years ago, there was no such thing as an MG car. But it immediately made a name for itself, becoming exceptionally active and making significant progress. The following is a brief account of its success story, which the readers may find interesting.

Initially, Mr. Morris (now known as Sir William Morris) not only had a large and thriving manufacturing plant in Cowley but also owned several car dealerships in Oxford, managed by Mr. Cecil Kimber. Mr. Kimber was skilled in manufacturing motorcycles, striving for perfection and speed. When he had the opportunity to manage car manufacturing, he applied his spirit of striving for excellence in motorcycles to cars. He strongly urged his superiors to devote his full efforts to improving the then-popular bullnose Morris Oxford car, to make it faster than other Morris cars. Although only six of these handcrafted cars were produced in the first year, the success of all subsequent great plans and the transformation of the Morris bullnose radiator into today's long style are based on this. As a result of Mr. Kimber's efforts, the new MG car was a success, unique and distinctive, with its own unapproachable characteristics.

Since then, improvements have been made step by step. Two years ago, through fortuitous circumstances, he acquired a state-of-the-art manufacturing plant, and a new company was formed, still managed by Mr. Kimber. Sir William remained a strong supporter. The new company was larger in scale and better equipped, and various new cars were launched one after another. In total, the factory produced three types of MG cars: the 17.7 horsepower six-cylinder MG, the 8 horsepower MG, and the MG Midget. In summary, the design and construction of MG cars are all based on "speed above all else" and "safe and fast" as their goals. It is no wonder that their performance is excellent and they are enthusiastically welcomed by the world.

Standard Nine Car Victory · 156

The automobile test held on March 4th of this year was initiated by Colonel Phillips and directed by the Royal Automobile Club. A total of 341 vehicles participated in the test, including powerful large cars and exquisite small cars. As a result of the test, the Standard Nine car driven by Mr. Stirling, ranked third, was one of the best performing and most effective vehicles in the preliminary round. It is true that there were many cars participating in the test that had good performance, but among them, only the Standard Nine Saloon driven by Mr. Oliver and the Standard Nine Saloon driven by Mr. Stirling, which won the third prize, stood out. This is truly an outstanding small vehicle in the modern automotive world.

Overseas Chatter

Automotive News from Abroad · Pei · 159

▲ Use of Safety Glass in Automobiles According to news from New York, in the recent automobile exhibition, many automobiles have used safety glass as an accessory. Among the thirty-three types of automobiles at the exhibition, eighteen were equipped with safety glass, and it was standard, customers could not freely replace it. In addition, the prices of various automobiles would slightly increase to adjust to the installation of safety glass. All types of automobiles with safety glass installed include the following brands: Packard, Studebaker, Pierce Arrow, Franklin, Willys-Knight, Willys Eight and Six, Chrysler, Dodge, DeSoto, Plymouth, Lincoln, LaSalle, Cadillac, Rolls-Royce, De Soto Airflow, Marmon Sixteen, etc. Each model of car has a safety glass installation, and most Ford models have been equipped with safety glass for several years now. Although several states in the United States require the use of safety glass by public regulation, the reason why manufacturers use this type of glass is due to consumer demand.

▲ Number of Automobiles in Spain The total number of automobiles in Spain is 60,113. On average, there is one automobile for every eighty residents. Among the provinces and cities, Barcelona has the highest number of automobiles, with 48,356 automobiles. Secondly, Madrid has 42,037 automobiles. Seville has 14,729 automobiles. Valencia has 12,460 automobiles. Among the provinces and cities, the area with the fewest automobiles is Ávila, which is in the mountainous area west of Madrid.

▲ One Gas Station per Mile The United States has a very developed automobile industry, so there are also many gas stations. According to Mr. Hedges, the vice president of the New York Automobile Club, there is an average of one gas station per mile of national highway. He said that the United States has 225,000 miles of national highways, and there are about 210,828 gas stations in the country. The total number of gas stations selling automobile fuel and lubricating oil includes 123,979 gas stations, 53,081 workshops, 743 parking lots, and 1,146 workshop and parking lot combinations. There are 131,877 merchants selling gasoline and lubricating oil. Among the above 210,826 gas stations, 178,949 only sell gasoline and lubricating oil. In 1929, the total sales amount was $2,506,015,489.

▲ Number of Transportation Automobiles in the United States In 1931, the total number of transportation automobiles used in the United States was 3,490,000, of which farmers accounted for 26% of the total. The total number of car owners was 2,530,000. There were 96,500 public buses. There were 17,000 combined school transportation automobiles. There were 49,000 combined school buses. There were 12,000 public buses for city streets. There were 5,000 public buses for steam railways. There were 270 public buses for city street railways. There were 80 public buses for steam railways. There were 85 railway transportation automobiles used as part of shipping services. There were 10,000 motor transportation vehicles used by steam railways. There were 9,492 motor transportation vehicles used by railway express agencies.

▲ Total Number of Automobiles Produced in the United States In 1931, the total number of automobiles and transportation vehicles produced in the United States and Canada was 2,460,000. Among them, there were 2,040,000 passenger cars and 420,000 motor transportation vehicles. There were 1,880,000 sedans produced, accounting for 92% of the automobiles. The total sales value of automobiles was $1,170,000,000. The total sales value of transportation automobiles was $260,000,000. The total combined value of automobiles and transportation automobiles was $1,430,000,000. The average retail price of automobiles was $765. The average retail price of transportation automobiles was $824. The number of tires exported was 51,000,000. The value of automobile parts was $341,000,000. The wholesale value of rubber tire patching was $325,000,000. The value of automobiles, parts, tires, and patching was $2,101,000,000.

▲ The Relationship between Automobiles and Various Industries The automobile industry is closely related to other industries. The special development of the automobile industry in the United States has had a profound impact on other industries. The automobile industry accounts for the largest consumption of gasoline, rubber, copper, iron, lubricating oil, glass, aluminum, lead, etc. In 1931, the number of automobiles transported by railway and water was 3,090,000. The automobile industry accounted for 83% of the rubber used. The automobile manufacturing industry accounted for 60% of the glass used. The automobile manufacturing industry accounted for 16% of the steel used. The automobile manufacturing industry accounted for 17% of the wood and hardwood used. The automobile manufacturing industry accounted for 14% of the copper used. The automobile manufacturing industry accounted for 26% of the lead used. The automobile manufacturing industry accounted for 17% of the aluminum used. The automobile manufacturing industry accounted for 30% of the nickel used. The automobile manufacturing industry accounted for 11% of the tin used. The automobile industry accounted for 8% of the zinc used. The automobile industry consumed 85% of the gasoline. In 1931, the automobile industry used a total of 342,000,000 barrels of gasoline. The automobile industry used 10,300,000 barrels of lubricating oil. The automobile industry accounted for 50% of the lubricating oil used. In 1931, the automobile industry used 649,700,000 pounds of raw rubber. In 1931, the cotton used in the manufacture of automobile tire wheels was 191,500,000 pounds.

Miscellaneous Records

Overview of the Dunlop Rubber Company · Yun · 160

Consider that most businesses, regardless of their industry, start small and simple, but through hard work, they eventually grow and their activities spread throughout the world. There are many such businesses, but among them, the Dunlop Rubber Company stands out as the one that has made the most rapid progress and achieved the most amazing results. Since Dr. J. B. Dunlop invented the pneumatic tire in 1888, more than forty years have passed. During this period, the company has worked hard to advance its business and has always been consistent, never slacking off. Therefore, its results have become better and its business has become more prosperous. Today, the company's factories are located on five continents, and its products are popular all over the world.

Given the Dunlop Company's grand scale and extensive activities, it is not easy to understand its details. However, a look at the following major aspects should give you a good idea of its situation.

Dunlop Company currently has 200,000 spindles, working day and night, to weave its famous combed textiles for the manufacture of tires.

Each year, Dunlop Company uses 40,000 tons of rubber. In the tropical regions, it has 100,000 acres of rubber plantations, and employs no less than 15,000 workers just to do this kind of work.

The total number of Dunlop distributors around the world reaches 60,000 households, all dedicated to selling Dunlop tires and serving their customers.

In total, there are approximately 30 million Dunlop tires of various types in use on roads around the world. Even more remarkably, every two and a quarter seconds, someone somewhere in the world buys a Dunlop tire.

Dunlop Rubber Company is a manufacturer of various types of tires, ranging from large tires used by large bomber aircraft and commercial aircraft to small tires used by children's prams. Dunlop Company can be proud to say that whenever movement depends on rubber, there is a Dunlop tire to suit the purpose.

Dunlop Rubber Company pioneered the pneumatic automobile tire, so it was also the first to introduce the pneumatic rickshaw tire to China. Old-fashioned solid tires are now almost extinct in China.

Sir Henry Segrave drove his 1,000 horsepower Sunbeam racing car to a record speed of 203.8 miles per hour at Daytona Beach on March 29, 1927. The tires used on the car were specially made by the Dunlop Company at the request of Sir Segrave. Sir Malcolm Campbell achieved a record of 260 miles per hour in 1931, also using Dunlop tires.

In addition to tires, Dunlop Company is also a manufacturer of the famous Dunlop tennis balls and golf balls. At every competition in the United Kingdom, the winners use them happily. The balls used in the recent Chinese Open Golf Championship were also Dunlop products. In 1931, 23 countries selected Dunlop balls for their national championship competitions. Among the 22 countries participating in the Davis Cup competition, 19 countries, including the final, selected Dunlop balls. [I>Driving a 1932 Citroen sports car for a country outing is a lot of fun
